***heden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heden.html>heden</a> (4533)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:heden.html>heden</a></i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hude</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">huden</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hiudo</i>, a contraction of the instrumental phrase <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hiu dago</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">on this day</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The appearance of the vowel <i>-e-</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unusual, the expected form in modern Dutch would be <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">*<a href = vnd.unilang:huiden.html>huide</a>(n)</i>, compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huidig.html>huidig</a></i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">hiudu</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">hūdigu</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">heute</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">hjoed</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hēodæg</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heden.html>heden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>today</li>
<li>presently</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heden.html>heden</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>the present</li></ol>

***hedendaags.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hedendaags.html>hedendaags</a> (49380)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hedendages</i>, originally an adverb. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heden.html>heden</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s</i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">hedendag</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hedendaags.html>hedendaags</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hedendaags.html>hedendaagser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hedendaags.html>hedendaags</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">hedendaagst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>current, contemporary, modern
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">In <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hedendaags.html>hedendaagse</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:samenleving.html>samenleving</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaats</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> revolverhelden.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> no room for gunslingers in <b>modern day</b> society.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">modern</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἡδονή</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hēdonḗ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pleasure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>  + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ist</i>.

</p>

***heel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a> (130)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hêel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hēl</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hailaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heler.html>heler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">heelst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>complete, full, whole</li>
<li>unbroken, undamaged, untarnished</li>
<li>big, enormous, significant</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_3">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gans.html>gans</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:volledig.html>volledig</a></span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geheel.html>geheel</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:helen.html>helen</a></span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heil.html>heil</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>very</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Although an adverb, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a></i> may be inflected as well (<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hele.html>hele</a></i>) to match the following adjective, by analogy with the inflection of adjectives in Dutch.
</p><p>. For example, both of these sentences are correct:
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>grote</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <b>very</b> large tree.</span></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hele.html>hele</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>grote</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <b>very</b> large tree.</span></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<p>The latter form may be regarded as informal and less appropriate for formal writing.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:henen.html>henen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">away from here, hence</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>

***heer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heer.html>heer</a> (762)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hêre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hērro</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hēro</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">hēriro</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">hērro</i>, the comparative form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">hēr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">noble, venerable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">hehr</i>), by analogy with Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">senior</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">elder</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The Old High German word originally meant "grey, grey-haired", and descends from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hairaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grey</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, making it cognate with English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hoar</i>, Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hárr</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heer.html>heer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heren.html>heren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heertje.html>heertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>lord; master</li>
<li>gentleman</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:heerlijkheid.html>heerlijkheid</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>

<li><a href = vnd.unilang:adellijke.html>adellijke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:legereenheid.html>legereenheid</a>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heersen.html>heersen</a> (6553)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hêerschen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to command, rule</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">herrschen</i> (Early New High German). <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:heffen.html>heffen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:heffen.html>heffen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*habjaną</i>, a class 6 strong verb with j-present, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kh₂pyéti</i>, from the root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*keh₂p-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to seize</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***heftig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heftig.html>heftig</a> (5302)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>16th c., borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:heftig.html>heftig</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">heftec</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">heiftec</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">heiftig</i>. Can be analyzed as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heft.html>heft</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">control</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-y</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heftig.html>heftig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heftiger.html>heftiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">heftigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fierce, severe</li>
<li>violent</li>
<li>passionate</li>
<li>impetuous, impulsive</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">heftigheid</span></li></ul>

***heg.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heg.html>heg</a> (23160)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hegge</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hegga</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*haggju</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hedge</i> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hecke</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kagʰyo-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kagʰyóm</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">enclosure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cohum</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">cae</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heidens.html>heidens</a> (30517)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heiden.html>heiden</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s</i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heidens.html>heidens</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heidens.html>heidenser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heidens.html>heidens</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">heidenst</b>)

<ol><li>pagan <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">pertaining to paganism</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

<li>gentile <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">pertaining to Non-Jews</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> uncivilised, heathen</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> immense, enormous</li></ol>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hei.html>hei</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">kneuter</i>. The sense “bumpkin” may be due to association with unrelated <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">keuter</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">keuterboer</i>.

***heiligheid.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heiligheid.html>heiligheid</a> (10119)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">heilichede</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heilig.html>heilig</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-heid</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heimlich.html>heimlich</a> (40726)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:heimlich.html>heimlich</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">heimelich</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">heimilīh</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*haimalīkaz</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Heim</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">-lich</i>. ***hein.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hein.html>hein</a> (22234)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hein.html>hein</a></i>, from the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:heinen.html>heinen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to physically demarcate lands</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:heinen.html>heinen</a></i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:omheinen.html>omheinen</a></i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hein.html>hein</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heinen.html>heinen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hein.html>heintje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>physical demarcation between fields or <a href = vnd.unilang:yards.html>yards</a>, like a fence, wall or ditch.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haag.html>haag</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heg.html>heg</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hagen.html>hagen</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behagen.html>behagen</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">omhagen</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heinen.html>heinen</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">heining</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:omheinen.html>omheinen</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:omheining.html>omheining</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">ijzerenheinig</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hein.html>hein</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heinen.html>heinen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hein.html>heintje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>skinny person</li>
<li>skinny horse</li>
<li>personification of death</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heist.html>heist</a> (69673)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Pronunciation variation of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hoist</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:heist.html>heist</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">heists</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A robbery or burglary, especially from an institution such as a bank or museum.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b> August 21,  “A brazen <a href = vnd.unilang:heist.html>heist</a> in Paris  | print version: <i>International New York Times</i>, 22 August 2014, p. 8 | ”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_New_York_Times" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The New York Times">The New York Times</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2014/08/22/opinion/a-brazen-heist-in-paris.html">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The audacious hijacking in Paris of a <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> carrying the baggage of a Saudi prince to his private jet <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> obviously an embarrassment to the French capital, whose ultra-high-end <a href = vnd.unilang:boutiques.html>boutiques</a> have suffered a spate of <b>heists</b> in recent months.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A fiction genre in which a <a href = vnd.unilang:heist.html>heist</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> central to the plot.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2002</b>,  <cite>Theatre Record</cite>, page 1177:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a conventional <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heist.html>heist</a></b> play in which the drama <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> created less through the characters' actions than through the fact of one of them having a gun.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>2008</b> March 6, Robert Wilonsky, "Fast and Loose", <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Riverfront_Times" class="extiw" title="w:Riverfront Times">Riverfront Times</a></i> volume 32 number 10, page 28,
<dl><dd><i>The Bank Job</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also the first proper Jason Statham movie since his days banging about in Guy Ritchie's early <b>heists</b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b>,  Daryl Lee,  <cite>The <a href = vnd.unilang:heist.html>Heist</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>Film</a>: Stealing With Style</cite>, page 69:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The crew resemble typical <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heist.html>heist</a></b> characters[.]</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:heist.html>heist</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">heists</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">heisting</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">heisted</b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heks.html>heks</a> (2241)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hexe</i>; ousted <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hagetesse</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hagetisse</i>. From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hagatusjǭ</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hægtesse</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>witch</li></ol>

***hel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hel.html>hel</a> (910)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:helle.html>helle</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hella</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*haljō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱel-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cover, hide, conceal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hel.html>hel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hellen.html>hellen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hel.html>helletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion<span class="ib-comma">,</span> mythology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Hell, an infernal afterlife.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hoop</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:branden.html>branden</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hel.html>hel</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I hope you will burn in <b>hell</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:poel.html>poel</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">jammerpoel</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A terrible place or ordeal.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maakte.html>maakte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daarmee.html>daarmee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hel.html>hel</a></b>.</i>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">helet</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hero, <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>, warrior</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:helt.html>helt</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*haliþaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>, hero</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, further etymology unknown.

***helder.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:helder.html>helder</a> (2777)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heller.html>heller</a></i>, derived from or related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hel.html>hel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bright</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, though the origin of the suffix <i><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unknown.<sup id="cite_ref-Philippa_EWN_2009_1-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-Philippa_EWN_2009-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>

<ul><li><b>2018</b> 25 June, Carolien Roelants, “Goed <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuws.html>nieuws</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> Jemen plus <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> Hollandse kortzichtigheid”, nrc.nl:

<dl><dd>Very good, very expensive coffee, especially destined for the Asiatic market, for “Europe <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> more sensitive to the price”, he says elegantly.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***helen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:helen.html>helen</a> (2213)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hêlen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hēlen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hailijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:helen.html>helen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ergative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to heal.
<ul><li><b>1805</b>, IJsbrand <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Hamelsveld (tr.), Jeremiah 46, 11, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bijbel.html>Bijbel</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> Hebreeuwsch. <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oude.html>Oude</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:testament.html>Testament</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:johannes.html>Johannes</a> Allart (publ.), page 908.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>Ga</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrij.html>vrij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naa.html>naa</a> Gileäd! <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> balzemen <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:halen.html>halen</a>, / Egijptisch <a href = vnd.unilang:maagd.html>maagd</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:vergeefs.html>Vergeefs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bereidt.html>bereidt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a> artzenij; / <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>Daar</a> 's <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:genezen.html>genezen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:helen.html>helen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uw.html>uw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wonden.html>wonden</a>!</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Go off to Gilead to get some balms, / Egyptian virgin! In vain you prepare medicine; / There <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> no curing, no <b>healing</b> for your wounds!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wonden.html>wonden</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:heelt.html>heelt</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The time that heals all wounds.</span></dd></dl></div><small> (<a href = vnd.unilang:marco.html>Marco</a> Borsato  |  <a href = vnd.unilang:wereld.html>Wereld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zonder.html>Zonder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jou.html>Jou</a>) </small></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hēlen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*helan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*helaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hide, conceal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱéleti</i>. The modern sense <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> probably borrowed from early modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">hehlen</i>.
</p>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebt.html>hebt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spullen.html>spullen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:geheeld.html>geheeld</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:strafbaar.html>strafbaar</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You have <b>accepted</b> those <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stolen.html>stolen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> and that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> illegal.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:helen.html>helen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to heal, to cure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos"><a href = vnd.unilang:agent.html>agent</a> noun suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:helen.html>helen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to receive, to fence</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heling.html>heling</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heling.html>helingen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fencing (buying of <a href = vnd.unilang:stolen.html>stolen</a> goods)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:helen.html>helen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to heal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.

<p><b>hell</b>
</p>

<dl><dd>«Since the very beginning of the religion, <b>hell</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> known to be an eternal damnation.»

***hellen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hellen.html>hellen</a> (40725)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:helden.html>helden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:helden.html>helden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*halþijaną</i>. The loss of the <i>d</i> occurred by reanalysis of the past tense form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:helde.html>helde</a></i> as consisting of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">hel-de</i> rather than <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">held-de</i>.

***hellfire.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hellfire.html>hellfire</a> (75450)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:helle.html>helle</a> fire</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">helever</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hellefȳr</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hell</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fire</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">helfjoer</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hellfire.html>hellfire</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hellevuur.html>hellevuur</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hellfire.html>hellfire</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Höllenfeuer</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hellfire.html>hellfire</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hellfire.html>hellfire</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hellfires</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The fire of Hell.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Fire produced by the Devil, or a similar supernatural creature connected to Hell.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A fire that burns with unusual heat or ferocity.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hellfire.html>hellfire</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:hellfire.html>hellfire</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:hellfire.html>hellfire</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Or or relating to a violent, apocalyptic and ultimate day of reckoning and judgment; usually characterizing a form of Christian preaching.
<ul><li><b>1902</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_James" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William James">William James</a>, <i>The Varieties of Religious Experience</i>, Lectures 4 amp; 5:
<dl><dd>The advance of liberalism, so-called, in Christianity, during the past fifty years, may fairly be called a victory of healthy-mindedness within the church <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the morbidness with which the old <b>hell-fire</b> theology <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> more harmoniously related.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2005</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sang_Hyun_Lee" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Sang Hyun Lee"><a href = vnd.unilang:sang.html>Sang</a> Hyun Lee</a>, <i>The Princeton Companion to <a href = vnd.unilang:jonathan.html>Jonathan</a> Edwards</i> (University of Princeton Press), p. 253:
<dl><dd>Sermons such as <i>The Eternity of Hell Torments</i> and <i>The Future Punishment of the Wicked Unavoidable and Intolerable</i>, as well as several manuscript examples, serve to mark the distinction between a true <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hellfire.html>hellfire</a></b> sermon and the proto-eschatological <a href = vnd.unilang:concerns.html>concerns</a> of <i>Sinners [in the Hands of an Angry <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a>]</i>, consumed as it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> with the here and now.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>
